		<div class="tan-catalog" style="display: none;">
            <div class="tan-catalog-con">
                <h4>未观看过的时间段</h4>
                <i class="btn_close"></i>
                <ul></ul>
                <div class="tan-catalog-info clearfix">
                    <i></i>
                    <span>当视频课程观看进度不完整或因网络异常造成进
                        度统计不完整时，需要补看才能完成学习。</span>
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>
	</div>
</div>


<script>
    // 关闭补看弹窗
    $(".btn_close").on("click",function(){
        $(".tan-catalog").hide()
    })

    // 补看点击事件
    $(".repar_view").on("click",function(){
        var videoId = $(this).data("video-id").toString();
        var backStatus = $(this).data("back-id");
        var cwareID = pageData.cwareID;
        getVideoCatchInfo(cwareID,videoId,backStatus);
    })

    // 获取补看数据
    function getVideoCatchInfo(cwareID,videoID,backStatus){
        $.getJSON(pageData.basePath+"/video/videoPlay/getVideoCatchInfo.shtm",
            {
                cwareID:cwareID,
                videoID:videoID,
                r:Math.random()
            },
            function(data){
                var videoRefID = "&#39;" + "1.1." + cwareID + "." + videoID + "&#39;";
                var timeMap;
                if(data){
                    timeMap = data;
                }else{
                    timeMap = JSON.parse(pageData.catchTimeMap);
                }
                var timeStr = timeMap[videoID];
                if(timeStr){
                    var timeArray = timeStr.split(",");
                    // 清空原来的内容
                    $(".tan-catalog-con ul").empty();
                    // 根据数组动态生成
                    timeArray.forEach(function (time) {
                        var startTime = time.split("-")[0];
                        var endTime = time.split("-")[1];
                        var li = "<li>";
                        li += "<span class='flV2'>" + time + "</span>"
                        li += "<em class='fr' onclick='playVideoByRefId(" + videoRefID +  ',' + "&#39;" + startTime + "&#39;" + ',' + backStatus + ',' + "&#39;" + endTime + "&#39;" + ")'></em>";
                        li += "</li>";
                        $(".tan-catalog-con ul").append(li);
                    });
                }
                // 显示弹窗
                $(".tan-catalog").show();
            }
        );
    }

    // 播放器跳转方法
    function playVideoByRefId(videoRefId,startTime,backStatus,endTime){
        cdelvideo.flashapi.playVideoByRefId(videoRefId,startTime,backStatus,endTime);
    }

	//20220505 add 提示
	var testLeftRoll = function(id,rollId){
		if($(id).length && $(id).length>0){
			var _id = $(id),
				_roll = _id.find(rollId),
				id_w = _id.width(),
				roll_w = _roll.width();
			if(roll_w > id_w){
				_roll.append(_roll.find('p').clone()).width(roll_w*2)
				var num = 0,
				goLeft = function() {
					if (num == '-' + roll_w){
						num = 0;
					}
					num -= 1;
					_roll.css({
						left: num
					})
				}
				//设置滚动速度
				var timer = setInterval(goLeft, 40);
				//设置鼠标经过时滚动停止
				_id.hover(function() {
					clearInterval(timer);
				},
				function() {
					timer = setInterval(goLeft, 40);
				})
			}
		}
	}
	setTimeout(function (){
		testLeftRoll('.clc-announcement-main','.clc-announcement-roll');
	},2000);

	//打开课件更新题型
	$('.viewBtn').click(function(){
		$('.updatePromptBox,.updateMask').show();
	})
	$('.updatePromptBox .close-box').click(function(){
		$('.updatePromptBox,.updateMask').hide();
	})

<script>
    // 关闭补看弹窗
    $(".btn_close").on("click",function(){
        $(".tan-catalog").hide()
    })

    // 补看点击事件
    $(".repar_view").on("click",function(){
        var videoId = $(this).data("video-id").toString();
        var backStatus = $(this).data("back-id");
        var cwareID = pageData.cwareID;
        getVideoCatchInfo(cwareID,videoId,backStatus);
    })

    // 获取补看数据
    function getVideoCatchInfo(cwareID,videoID,backStatus){
        $.getJSON(pageData.basePath+"/video/videoPlay/getVideoCatchInfo.shtm",
            {
                cwareID:cwareID,
                videoID:videoID,
                r:Math.random()
            },
            function(data){
                var videoRefID = "&#39;" + "1.1." + cwareID + "." + videoID + "&#39;";
                var timeMap;
                if(data){
                    timeMap = data;
                }else{
                    timeMap = JSON.parse(pageData.catchTimeMap);
                }
                var timeStr = timeMap[videoID];
                if(timeStr){
                    var timeArray = timeStr.split(",");
                    // 清空原来的内容
                    $(".tan-catalog-con ul").empty();
                    // 根据数组动态生成
                    timeArray.forEach(function (time) {
                        var startTime = time.split("-")[0];
                        var endTime = time.split("-")[1];
                        var li = "<li>";
                        li += "<span class='flV2'>" + time + "</span>"
                        li += "<em class='fr' onclick='playVideoByRefId(" + videoRefID +  ',' + "&#39;" + startTime + "&#39;" + ',' + backStatus + ',' + "&#39;" + endTime + "&#39;" + ")'></em>";
                        li += "</li>";
                        $(".tan-catalog-con ul").append(li);
                    });
                }
                // 显示弹窗
                $(".tan-catalog").show();
            }
        );
    }

    // 播放器跳转方法
    function playVideoByRefId(videoRefId,startTime,backStatus,endTime){
        cdelvideo.flashapi.playVideoByRefId(videoRefId,startTime,backStatus,endTime);
    }

	//20220505 add 提示
	var testLeftRoll = function(id,rollId){
		if($(id).length && $(id).length>0){
			var _id = $(id),
				_roll = _id.find(rollId),
				id_w = _id.width(),
				roll_w = _roll.width();
			if(roll_w > id_w){
				_roll.append(_roll.find('p').clone()).width(roll_w*2)
				var num = 0,
				goLeft = function() {
					if (num == '-' + roll_w){
						num = 0;
					}
					num -= 1;
					_roll.css({
						left: num
					})
				}
				//设置滚动速度
				var timer = setInterval(goLeft, 40);
				//设置鼠标经过时滚动停止
				_id.hover(function() {
					clearInterval(timer);
				},
				function() {
					timer = setInterval(goLeft, 40);
				})
			}
		}
	}
	setTimeout(function (){
		testLeftRoll('.clc-announcement-main','.clc-announcement-roll');
	},2000);

	//打开课件更新题型
	$('.viewBtn').click(function(){
		$('.updatePromptBox,.updateMask').show();
	})
	$('.updatePromptBox .close-box').click(function(){
		$('.updatePromptBox,.updateMask').hide();
	})

<script>
	var showPointTest = function (pointVideoLen, pointOpenType) {
		window.testController.showPoint4Click(pointVideoLen, pointOpenType);
	}

	var closeTest = function () {
	}

	var csPop = function (el,nodeID,userID,cwareID,videoID) {
		var cwareID = pageData.cwareID;
		var videoID = pageData.videoID;
        $.getJSON(pageData.basePath+'/testPop/getPointFlag.shtm',{
            cwareID:cwareID,
            videoID:videoID,
            r:Math.random()
        },function(data){
			// 控制div显示（0 都不显示设置选项，1 都显示显示，2 显示知识点测试，3 显示单元测试）
			var test = data[0];
			console.log(test);
			// 两个设置选项
			var setPointTest = $('#setPointTest');
			var setUnitTest = $('#setUnitTest');
			switch (test.settingFlag) {
				case 1:
					setPointTest.show();
					setUnitTest.show();
					break;
				case 2:
					setPointTest.show();
					setUnitTest.hide();
					break;
				case 3:
					setPointTest.hide();
					setUnitTest.show();
					break;
				default:
					setPointTest.hide();
					setUnitTest.hide();
					break;
			}
            $("#zPopFlag1").addClass("on");
            $("#dPopFlag1").addClass("on");
			$("#tPopFlag1").addClass("on");

            for (var i = 0, len = data.length; i < len; i++) {
                var test = data[i];
                var currOpenType = test.pointOpenType;
                switch (currOpenType) {
                    case "z": //知识点测试
                        var chickID = test.pointFlag == 0?"zPopFlag0":"zPopFlag1"
                        $("#"+chickID).addClass("on").siblings('li').removeClass('on');
                        break;
                    case "d": //单元测试
                        var chickID = test.pointFlag == 0?"dPopFlag0":"dPopFlag1"
                        $("#"+chickID).addClass("on").siblings('li').removeClass('on');
                        break;
					case "t": //知识点练习
						var chickID = test.pointFlag == 0?"tPopFlag0":"tPopFlag1"
						$("#"+chickID).addClass("on").siblings('li').removeClass('on');
						break;
                    default :
                        $("#zPopFlag1").addClass("on");
                        $("#dPopFlag1").addClass("on");
                        $("#tPopFlag1").addClass("on");
                        break;
                }
            }

        });
		var _this = $("." + el);
		var myHeight = _this.height();
		_this.css("marginTop", -myHeight / 2)
		$(".mask").show();
		_this.show();
	}

</script>

<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>1.下列各项中，可全额在企业所得税税前扣除的有（　）。<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>A.航空企业空中保卫员训练费用<br>

<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>D.技术先进型服务企业的职工教育经费<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>E.符合条件的软件生产企业单独进行核算的职工培训费用<br>
</td></tr><tr id="tr_show_6255865_1" class="picShow class_tr_show_6255865_1" style="display: block;"><td colspan="3" style="font-size: 12px;"><img src="http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer01.gif" style="cursor:pointer;" onclick="showAnswer('6255865_1');"></td></tr><tr id="tr_hide_6255865_1" class="jyTxt class_tr_6255865_1" style="display:none;"><td class="jyTxtHideTd" colspan="3" style="background-image: url(&quot;http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer04.gif&quot;); font-size: 12px;"><img src="http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer02.gif" style="cursor:pointer;" onclick="hideAnswer('6255865_1');"></td></tr><tr id="tr_answer_6255865_1" class="jyTxt class_tr_6255865_1" style="display:none;"><td class="jyTxtAnswerTd" style="background-image: url(&quot;http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer03.gif&quot;); background-repeat: repeat-y; width: 16px; font-size: 12px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" style="text-align: left; width: 98%; font-size: 12px;">
『正确答案』ABE<br>
『答案解析』选项A，航空企业实际发生的飞行员养成费、飞行训练费、乘务训练费、空中保卫员训练费等空勤训练费用，可以作为航空企业运输成本在税前扣除。选项B，核力发电企业为培养核电厂操纵员发生的培养费用，可作为企业的发电成本在税前扣除。选项C、D，高新技术企业和技术先进型服务企业，发生的培训费用，属于职工教育经费，不超过工资、薪金总额8％的部分，准予在计算企业所得税应纳税所得额时扣除。选项E，符合条件软件企业的职工培训费用，单独进行核算并按实际发生额在计算应纳税所得额时扣除。<br>
</td></tr></tbody></table>
</li></ul><a href="javascript:void(0)" onclick="cdelvideo.flashapi.seekVideo('00:00:01');" class="play-btn" title="点击跳到本段播放(00:00:01)"></a></div></div><div class="ask-box"><div class="commonAsk-wrap"><a href="javascript:void(0)" onclick="openAiFaqWithLecture('NODE04763100100200000102', '1002');" class="ask-btn" id="divask_NODE04763100100200000102" style="display: none; float: right; vertical-align: top; line-height: 22px; font-size: 12px; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); position: relative; font-weight: normal; padding: 0px 8px; background: rgb(255, 164, 67); border-radius: 6px; text-decoration: none;">针对本讲义进行提问</a></div><div class="memoDiv" id="div_NODE04763100100200000102" ondblclick="cdelvideo.flashapi.seekVideo('00:00:40');" style="cursor:pointer;" title="双击跳到本段播放(00:00:40)"><ul><li style="word-break: break-all; font-size: 12px;">
<table class="tableA" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0"><tbody><tr><td colspan="3" style="font-size: 12px;">
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>2.企业从县级以上各级人民政府财政部门及其他部门取得的应计入收入总额的财政性资金，作为不征税收入，应同时符合的条件有（　）。<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>A.企业能够提供规定资金专项用途的资金拨付文件<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>B.资金使用的具体情况每年必须报上级主管部门备案<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>C.企业对该资金以及以该资金发生的支出单独进行核算<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>D.该资金不得用于资本性支出<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>E.财政部门对该资金有专门的资金管理办法或具体管理要求<br>
</td></tr><tr id="tr_show_6255866_1" class="picShow class_tr_show_6255866_1" style="display: block;"><td colspan="3" style="font-size: 12px;"><img src="http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer01.gif" style="cursor:pointer;" onclick="showAnswer('6255866_1');"></td></tr><tr id="tr_hide_6255866_1" class="jyTxt class_tr_6255866_1" style="display:none;"><td class="jyTxtHideTd" colspan="3" style="background-image: url(&quot;http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer04.gif&quot;); font-size: 12px;"><img src="http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer02.gif" style="cursor:pointer;" onclick="hideAnswer('6255866_1');"></td></tr><tr id="tr_answer_6255866_1" class="jyTxt class_tr_6255866_1" style="display:none;"><td class="jyTxtAnswerTd" style="background-image: url(&quot;http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer03.gif&quot;); background-repeat: repeat-y; width: 16px; font-size: 12px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" style="text-align: left; width: 98%; font-size: 12px;">
『正确答案』ACE<br>
『答案解析』企业从县级以上各级人民政府财政部门及其他部门取得的应计入收入总额的财政性资金，凡同时符合以下条件的，可以作为不征税收入，在计算应纳税所得额时从收入总额中减除：①企业能够提供规定资金专项用途的资金拨付文件（选项A）；②财政部门或其他拨付资金的政府部门对该资金有专门的资金管理办法或具体管理要求（选项E）；③企业对该资金以及以该资金发生的支出单独进行核算（选项C）。<br>
</td></tr></tbody></table>

<table class="tableA" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0"><tbody><tr><td colspan="3" style="font-size: 12px;">
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>3.下列关于企业手续费及佣金支出税前扣除规定的表述中，正确的有（　）。<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>A.保险企业按当年全部保费收入的18％计算扣除限额<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>B.保险企业按当年全部保费收入扣除退保金等后余额的18％计算扣除限额<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>C.电信企业在发展客户、拓展业务等过程中实际发生的相关手续费及佣金支出，不超过企业当年收入总额5％的部分，准予在税前扣除<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>D.企业为发行权益性证券支付给有关证券承销机构的手续费及佣金不得在税前扣除<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>E.企业不得将手续费及佣金支出计入回扣、业务提成、返利、进场费等费用<br>

<table class="tableA" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0"><tbody><tr><td colspan="3" style="font-size: 12px;">
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>4.根据企业所得税法的规定，下列关于无形资产的税务处理正确的有（　）。<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>A.通过债务重组方式取得的无形资产，以该资产的公允价值和支付的相关税费为计税基础<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>B.无形资产的摊销，采取直线法计算<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>C.自创商誉的摊销年限，一般情况不得低于10年<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>D.企事业单位购进软件，凡符合无形资产确认条件的，可以按照无形资产进行核算，其摊销年限可以适当缩短，最短可为3年<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>E.外购商誉的支出，在企业整体转让或者清算时，准予扣除<br>
</td></tr><tr id="tr_show_6255868_1" class="picShow class_tr_show_6255868_1" style="display: block;"><td colspan="3" style="font-size: 12px;"><img src="http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer01.gif" style="cursor:pointer;" onclick="showAnswer('6255868_1');"></td></tr><tr id="tr_hide_6255868_1" class="jyTxt class_tr_6255868_1" style="display:none;"><td class="jyTxtHideTd" colspan="3" style="background-image: url(&quot;http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer04.gif&quot;); font-size: 12px;"><img src="http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer02.gif" style="cursor:pointer;" onclick="hideAnswer('6255868_1');"></td></tr><tr id="tr_answer_6255868_1" class="jyTxt class_tr_6255868_1" style="display:none;"><td class="jyTxtAnswerTd" style="background-image: url(&quot;http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer03.gif&quot;); background-repeat: repeat-y; width: 16px; font-size: 12px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" style="text-align: left; width: 98%; font-size: 12px;">
『正确答案』ABE<br>
『答案解析』选项C，企业自创商誉是不得计算摊销费用扣除的。选项D，企事业单位购进软件，凡符合固定资产或无形资产确认条件的，可以按照固定资产或无形资产进行核算，其折旧或摊销年限可以适当缩短，最短可为2年（含）。<br>
</td></tr></tbody></table>

<table class="tableA" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0"><tbody><tr><td colspan="3" style="font-size: 12px;">
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>5.根据企业所得税法的规定，下列各项中符合投资资产税务处理规定的有（　）。<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>A.企业对外投资期间，投资资产的成本在计算应纳税所得额时不得扣除<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>B.企业以非货币性资产对外投资，应对非货币性资产进行评估并按评估后的公允价值扣除计税基础后的余额，计算确认非货币性资产转让所得<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>C.企业以非货币性资产对外投资，应于投资协议生效并办理股权登记手续时，确认非货币性资产转让收入的实现<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>D.企业在转让或者处置投资资产时，投资资产的成本不得扣除<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>E.被投资企业取得非货币性资产的计税基础，应按非货币性资产的公允价值确定<br>
</td></tr><tr id="tr_show_6255869_1" class="picShow class_tr_show_6255869_1" style="display: block;"><td colspan="3" style="font-size: 12px;"><img src="http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer01.gif" style="cursor:pointer;" onclick="showAnswer('6255869_1');"></td></tr><tr id="tr_hide_6255869_1" class="jyTxt class_tr_6255869_1" style="display:none;"><td class="jyTxtHideTd" colspan="3" style="background-image: url(&quot;http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer04.gif&quot;); font-size: 12px;"><img src="http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer02.gif" style="cursor:pointer;" onclick="hideAnswer('6255869_1');"></td></tr><tr id="tr_answer_6255869_1" class="jyTxt class_tr_6255869_1" style="display:none;"><td class="jyTxtAnswerTd" style="background-image: url(&quot;http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer03.gif&quot;); background-repeat: repeat-y; width: 16px; font-size: 12px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" style="text-align: left; width: 98%; font-size: 12px;">
『正确答案』ABCE<br>
『答案解析』选项D，企业在转让或者处置投资资产时，投资资产的成本准予扣除。<br>
</td></tr></tbody></table>

<table class="tableA" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0"><tbody><tr><td colspan="3" style="font-size: 12px;">
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>6.下列关于房地产开发企业成本费用扣除的企业所得税处理中，正确的有（　）。<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>A.企业开发产品转为自用的，其实际使用时间累计未超过12个月又销售的，不得在税前扣除折旧费用<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>B.企业利用地下基础设施建成的停车场应作为公共配套设施处理<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>C.企业因国家无偿收回土地使用权而形成的损失，可作为财产损失按有关规定在税前扣除<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>D.企业支付给境外销售机构不超过委托销售收入20％的部分准予扣除<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>E.企业在房地产开发区内建造的学校应单独核算成本<br>

<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>10.根据个人所得税相关规定，下列关于企业转增股本的个人所得税表述中，正确的有（　）。<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>A.股份制企业用股票溢价发行收入形成的资本公积金转增股本，应按照“利息、股息、红利所得”计算个人所得税<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>B.全国范围内的中小高新技术企业以未分配利润向个人股东转增股本时，个人股东一次缴纳个人所得税确有困难的，在不超过5个公历年度内分期均匀缴纳<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>C.“新三板”挂牌的中小高新技术企业向个人股东转增股本（不含以股票发行溢价的资本公积转增股本），股东应缴纳的个人所得税，按股息红利差别化个人所得税政策执行<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>D.被投资企业以资本公积、盈余公积、未分配利润转增股本，个人股东已依法缴纳个人所得税的，以转增额和相关税费之和确认其新转增股本的股权原值<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>E.股东转让股权并取得现金收入的，该现金收入应优先用于缴纳尚未缴清的税款<br>
</td></tr><tr id="tr_show_6255874_1" class="picShow class_tr_show_6255874_1" style="display: block;"><td colspan="3" style="font-size: 12px;"><img src="http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer01.gif" style="cursor:pointer;" onclick="showAnswer('6255874_1');"></td></tr><tr id="tr_hide_6255874_1" class="jyTxt class_tr_6255874_1" style="display:none;"><td class="jyTxtHideTd" colspan="3" style="background-image: url(&quot;http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer04.gif&quot;); font-size: 12px;"><img src="http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer02.gif" style="cursor:pointer;" onclick="hideAnswer('6255874_1');"></td></tr><tr id="tr_answer_6255874_1" class="jyTxt class_tr_6255874_1" style="display:none;"><td class="jyTxtAnswerTd" style="background-image: url(&quot;http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer03.gif&quot;); background-repeat: repeat-y; width: 16px; font-size: 12px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" style="text-align: left; width: 98%; font-size: 12px;">
『正确答案』CDE<br>
『答案解析』选项A，股份制企业用资本公积金转增股本，不属于股息、红利性质的分配，对个人取得的转增股本数额，不作为个人所得，不征收个人所得税。资本公积金，是指股份制企业股票溢价发行收入所形成的资本公积金。选项B，自2016年1月1日起，全国范围内的中小高新技术企业以未分配利润、盈余公积、资本公积向个人股东转增股本时，个人股东一次缴纳个人所得税确有困难的，可根据实际情况自行制定分期缴税计划，在不超过5个公历年度内（含）分期缴纳，并将有关资料报主管税务机关备案。并没有分期均匀缴纳的规定。<br>
</td></tr></tbody></table>

<table class="tableA" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0"><tbody><tr><td colspan="3" style="font-size: 12px;">
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>11.根据个人所得税相关规定，下列转让行为应被视为股权转让收入明显偏低的有（　）。<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>A.申报的股权转让收入高于股权对应的净资产份额<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>B.申报的股权转让收入低于取得该股权所支付的价款和相关税费<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>C.不具有合理性的无偿转让股权<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>D.申报的股权转让收入低于相同或类似条件下同类行业的企业股权转让收入<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>E.申报的股权转让收入低于股权对应的净资产公允价值<br>
</td></tr><tr id="tr_show_6255875_1" class="picShow class_tr_show_6255875_1" style="display: block;"><td colspan="3" style="font-size: 12px;"><img src="http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer01.gif" style="cursor:pointer;" onclick="showAnswer('6255875_1');"></td></tr><tr id="tr_hide_6255875_1" class="jyTxt class_tr_6255875_1" style="display:none;"><td class="jyTxtHideTd" colspan="3" style="background-image: url(&quot;http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer04.gif&quot;); font-size: 12px;"><img src="http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer02.gif" style="cursor:pointer;" onclick="hideAnswer('6255875_1');"></td></tr><tr id="tr_answer_6255875_1" class="jyTxt class_tr_6255875_1" style="display:none;"><td class="jyTxtAnswerTd" style="background-image: url(&quot;http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer03.gif&quot;); background-repeat: repeat-y; width: 16px; font-size: 12px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" style="text-align: left; width: 98%; font-size: 12px;">
『正确答案』BCD<br>
『答案解析』符合下列情形之一，视为股权转让收入明显偏低：①申报的股权转让收入低于股权对应的净资产份额的；②申报的股权转让收入低于初始投资成本或低于取得该股权所支付的价款及相关税费的；③申报的股权转让收入低于相同或类似条件下同一企业同一股东或其他股东股权转让收入的；④申报的股权转让收入低于相同或类似条件下同类行业的企业股权转让收入的；⑤不具合理性的无偿让渡股权或股份；⑥主管税务机关认定的其他情形。<br>
</td></tr></tbody></table>

<table class="tableA" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0"><tbody><tr><td colspan="3" style="font-size: 12px;">
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>12.根据个人财产对外转移有关税收规定，下列说法正确的有（　）。<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>A.申请人拟转移的财产已取得完税凭证的，可直接向外汇管理部门提供完税凭证，无须向税务机关另外申请税收证明<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>B.申请人拟转移的财产总价值在人民币20万元以下的，无须向税务机关申请税收证明<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>C.开具税收证明的税务机关为县级或者县级以上税务局<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>D.申请人与纳税人姓名、名称不一致的，税务机关只对纳税人出具证明，申请人应向外汇管理部门提供其与纳税人关系的证明<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>E.申请人申请领取税收证明时，资料齐全的，税务机关应当在10日内开具税收证明<br>
</td></tr><tr id="tr_show_6255876_1" class="picShow class_tr_show_6255876_1" style="display: block;"><td colspan="3" style="font-size: 12px;"><img src="http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer01.gif" style="cursor:pointer;" onclick="showAnswer('6255876_1');"></td></tr><tr id="tr_hide_6255876_1" class="jyTxt class_tr_6255876_1" style="display:none;"><td class="jyTxtHideTd" colspan="3" style="background-image: url(&quot;http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer04.gif&quot;); font-size: 12px;"><img src="http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer02.gif" style="cursor:pointer;" onclick="hideAnswer('6255876_1');"></td></tr><tr id="tr_answer_6255876_1" class="jyTxt class_tr_6255876_1" style="display:none;"><td class="jyTxtAnswerTd" style="background-image: url(&quot;http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer03.gif&quot;); background-repeat: repeat-y; width: 16px; font-size: 12px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" style="text-align: left; width: 98%; font-size: 12px;">
『正确答案』ACD<br>
『答案解析』选项B，申请人拟转移的财产总价值在人民币15万元以下的，无须向税务机关申请税收证明。选项E，申请人申请领取税收证明时，资料齐全的，税务机关应当在15日内开具税收证明。<br>

<table class="tableA" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0"><tbody><tr><td colspan="3" style="font-size: 12px;">
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>13.下列关于税收情报交换的表述中，正确的有（　）。<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>A.我国从缔约国主管当局获取的税收情报可以作为税收执法行为的依据，并可以在诉讼程序中出示<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>B.税收情报交换在税收协定规定的权利和义务范围内进行<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>C.税收情报交换应在税收协定生效并执行以后进行，不能溯及税收协定生效并执行之前涉及的事项<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>D.税收情报交换税种范围通常针对具有所得（或财产）性质的税种<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>E.税收情报交换通过税收协定确定的主管当局或其授权代表进行<br>
</td></tr><tr id="tr_show_6255877_1" class="picShow class_tr_show_6255877_1" style="display: block;"><td colspan="3" style="font-size: 12px;"><img src="http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer01.gif" style="cursor:pointer;" onclick="showAnswer('6255877_1');"></td></tr><tr id="tr_hide_6255877_1" class="jyTxt class_tr_6255877_1" style="display:none;"><td class="jyTxtHideTd" colspan="3" style="background-image: url(&quot;http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer04.gif&quot;); font-size: 12px;"><img src="http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer02.gif" style="cursor:pointer;" onclick="hideAnswer('6255877_1');"></td></tr><tr id="tr_answer_6255877_1" class="jyTxt class_tr_6255877_1" style="display:none;"><td class="jyTxtAnswerTd" style="background-image: url(&quot;http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer03.gif&quot;); background-repeat: repeat-y; width: 16px; font-size: 12px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" style="text-align: left; width: 98%; font-size: 12px;">
『正确答案』ABE<br>
『答案解析』选项C，情报交换应在税收协定生效并执行以后进行，税收情报涉及的事项可以溯及税收协定生效并执行之前。选项D，除缔约国另有规定外，情报交换的范围一般为：①国家范围包括加入《多边税收征管互助公约》及与我国正式签订含有情报交换条款的税收协定并生效执行的国家；②税种范围通常涵盖所有税种，特别是具有所得（或财产）性质的税种；③人的范围，包括所有类型纳税人及相关主体；④地域范围，为全球范围内的涉税信息。<br>
</td></tr></tbody></table>

<table class="tableA" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0"><tbody><tr><td colspan="3" style="font-size: 12px;">
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>14.下列关于可转换债券转换为股权投资的税务处理表述中，正确的有（　）。<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>A.购买方企业购买可转换债券，在其持有期间按照约定利率取得的利息收入，应当依法申报缴纳企业所得税<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>B.购买方企业可转换债券转换为股票时，将应收未收利息一并转为股票的，该应收未收利息即使会计上未确认收入，税收上也应当作为当期利息收入申报纳税<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>C.发行方企业发生的可转换债券的利息，按照规定在税前扣除<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>D.发行方企业按照约定将购买方持有的可转换债券和应付未付利息一并转为股票的，其应付未付利息视同已支付，按照规定在税前扣除<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>E.购买方企业购买可转换债券，在其持有期间按照约定利率取得的利息收入，不征收企业所得税<br>
</td></tr><tr id="tr_show_6255878_1" class="picShow class_tr_show_6255878_1" style="display: block;"><td colspan="3" style="font-size: 12px;"><img src="http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer01.gif" style="cursor:pointer;" onclick="showAnswer('6255878_1');"></td></tr><tr id="tr_hide_6255878_1" class="jyTxt class_tr_6255878_1" style="display:none;"><td class="jyTxtHideTd" colspan="3" style="background-image: url(&quot;http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer04.gif&quot;); font-size: 12px;"><img src="http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer02.gif" style="cursor:pointer;" onclick="hideAnswer('6255878_1');"></td></tr><tr id="tr_answer_6255878_1" class="jyTxt class_tr_6255878_1" style="display:none;"><td class="jyTxtAnswerTd" style="background-image: url(&quot;http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer03.gif&quot;); background-repeat: repeat-y; width: 16px; font-size: 12px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" style="text-align: left; width: 98%; font-size: 12px;">
『正确答案』ABCD<br>
『答案解析』关于可转换债券转换为股权投资的税务处理要区分购买方和发行方来分析。<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>（1）购买方企业的税务处理：①购买方企业购买可转换债券，在其持有期间按照约定利率取得的利息收入，应当依法申报缴纳企业所得税。②购买方企业可转换债券转换为股票时，将应收未收利息一并转为股票的，该应收未收利息即使会计上未确认收入，税收上也应当作为当期利息收入申报纳税；转换后以该债券购买价、应收未收利息和支付的相关税费为该股票投资成本。<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>（2）发行方企业的税务处理：①发行方企业发生的可转换债券的利息，按照规定在税前扣除。②发行方企业按照约定将购买方持有的可转换债券和应付未付利息一并转为股票的，其应付未付利息视同已支付，按照规定在税前扣除。<br>
</td></tr></tbody></table>

<table class="tableA" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0"><tbody><tr><td colspan="3" style="font-size: 12px;">
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>15.下列合同或凭证中，不属于印花税征税范围的有（　）。<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>A.融资性售后回租业务中签订的购回租赁资产的合同<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>B.市人民政府及其所属部门按照行政管理权限收回或者补偿安置房地产书立的合同<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>C.分公司与分公司之间书立的作为执行计划使用的凭证<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>D.发行单位与订阅单位书立的征订凭证<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>E.企业之间书立的确定买卖关系、明确买卖双方权利义务的订单、要货单等单据，且未另外书立买卖合同<br>
</td></tr><tr id="tr_show_6255879_1" class="picShow class_tr_show_6255879_1" style="display: block;"><td colspan="3" style="font-size: 12px;"><img src="http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer01.gif" style="cursor:pointer;" onclick="showAnswer('6255879_1');"></td></tr><tr id="tr_hide_6255879_1" class="jyTxt class_tr_6255879_1" style="display:none;"><td class="jyTxtHideTd" colspan="3" style="background-image: url(&quot;http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer04.gif&quot;); font-size: 12px;"><img src="http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer02.gif" style="cursor:pointer;" onclick="hideAnswer('6255879_1');"></td></tr><tr id="tr_answer_6255879_1" class="jyTxt class_tr_6255879_1" style="display:none;"><td class="jyTxtAnswerTd" style="background-image: url(&quot;http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer03.gif&quot;); background-repeat: repeat-y; width: 16px; font-size: 12px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" style="text-align: left; width: 98%; font-size: 12px;">
『正确答案』ABC<br>
『答案解析』选项A、B、C，不属于印花税征税范围，不缴纳印花税。选项D，属于征税范围，暂免征收印花税。选项E，属于印花税征税范围，应当按规定缴纳印花税。<br>
</td></tr></tbody></table>

<table class="tableA" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0"><tbody><tr><td colspan="3" style="font-size: 12px;">
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>16.下列属于车船税征税范围的有（　）。<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>A.挂车<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>B.排量为50毫升的摩托车<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>C.混凝土泵车<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>D.车速大于每小时20公里的轮式工程机械车<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>E.长度小于90米用于游览观光的游艇<br>
</td></tr><tr id="tr_show_6255880_1" class="picShow class_tr_show_6255880_1" style="display: block;"><td colspan="3" style="font-size: 12px;"><img src="http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer01.gif" style="cursor:pointer;" onclick="showAnswer('6255880_1');"></td></tr><tr id="tr_hide_6255880_1" class="jyTxt class_tr_6255880_1" style="display:none;"><td class="jyTxtHideTd" colspan="3" style="background-image: url(&quot;http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer04.gif&quot;); font-size: 12px;"><img src="http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer02.gif" style="cursor:pointer;" onclick="hideAnswer('6255880_1');"></td></tr><tr id="tr_answer_6255880_1" class="jyTxt class_tr_6255880_1" style="display:none;"><td class="jyTxtAnswerTd" style="background-image: url(&quot;http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer03.gif&quot;); background-repeat: repeat-y; width: 16px; font-size: 12px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" style="text-align: left; width: 98%; font-size: 12px;">
『正确答案』ACDE<br>
『答案解析』选项B，无论采用何种驱动方式，最高设计车速大于每小时50公里，或者使用内燃机，其排量大于50毫升的两轮或者三轮摩托车，属于车船税征税范围。<br>

<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>A.纳税人缴纳契税后因新建商品房实际交付面积小于合同约定面积需要退还房价款的，可以依照有关规定申请退税<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>B.需在土地、房屋所在地缴纳契税<br>

<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>A.占用园地、林地、草地、农田水利用地、养殖水面、渔业水域滩涂从事非农业建设的，适用税额可以适当低于税法规定的适用税额，但降低的部分不得超过30％<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>B.耕地占用税减免优惠实行“自行判别、申报享受、有关资料留存备查”办理方式<br>

<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>D.耕地占用税采用地区差别比例税率<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>E.因挖损、污染等损毁耕地的，纳税义务发生时间为自然资源、农业农村等相关部门认定损毁耕地的当日<br>

<br><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span><strong>三、计算题</strong><br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>1.位于某市郊区的物流公司（小型微利企业）占地面积共计20 000平方米，其中，办公区占地18 000平方米，职工医院占地600平方米，幼儿园占地400平方米，内部绿化区占地1 000平方米。2024年发生以下占地情形：<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>（1）经有关部门批准，3月占用耕地20 000平方米用于建设大宗商品仓储设施，当月收到办理占用耕地手续的书面通知并签订土地使用权出让合同，政府减免土地出让金1 800万元、市政建设配套费150万元后，公司实际缴纳出让金1 200万元，另支付土地补偿费、青苗补偿和土地附着物补偿费共500万元。<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>（2）4月底无偿使用某免税单位占地面积为6 000平方米的房产，用于存储大宗商品，使用期一年。<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>（注：当地城镇土地使用税年税额为6元/平方米，耕地占用税税额为20元/平方米，契税税率为3％，该企业享受“六税两费”减半征收优惠。）<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>要求：根据上述资料，回答下列问题。<br>
<table class="tableA" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0"><tbody><tr><td colspan="3" style="font-size: 12px;">
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>（1）2024年该物流公司占用耕地应缴纳耕地占用税（　）万元。<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>A.20<br><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>B.33<br><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>C.40<br><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>D.30<br>
</td></tr><tr id="tr_show_6255885_1" class="picShow class_tr_show_6255885_1" style="display: block;"><td colspan="3" style="font-size: 12px;"><img src="http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer01.gif" style="cursor:pointer;" onclick="showAnswer('6255885_1');"></td></tr><tr id="tr_hide_6255885_1" class="jyTxt class_tr_6255885_1" style="display:none;"><td class="jyTxtHideTd" colspan="3" style="background-image: url(&quot;http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer04.gif&quot;); font-size: 12px;"><img src="http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer02.gif" style="cursor:pointer;" onclick="hideAnswer('6255885_1');"></td></tr><tr id="tr_answer_6255885_1" class="jyTxt class_tr_6255885_1" style="display:none;"><td class="jyTxtAnswerTd" style="background-image: url(&quot;http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer03.gif&quot;); background-repeat: repeat-y; width: 16px; font-size: 12px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" style="text-align: left; width: 98%; font-size: 12px;">
『正确答案』A<br>
『答案解析』耕地占用税以纳税人实际占用的耕地面积为计税依据，该物流公司就3月占用的耕地应缴纳耕地占用税＝20 000×20×50％÷10 000＝20（万元）。<br>

<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>A.36<br><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>B.105<br><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>C.109.5<br><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>D.51<br>

『正确答案』C<br>
『答案解析』应缴纳契税＝（1 800＋150＋1 200＋500）×3％＝109.5（万元）。<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>『得分关键』出让国有土地使用权的，其契税计税价格为承受人为取得该土地使用权而支付的全部经济利益。以协议方式出让的，其契税计税价格为成交价格。成交价格包括土地出让金、土地补偿费、安置补助费地上附着物和青苗补偿费、拆迁补偿费、市政建设配套费等承受者应支付的货币、实物、无形资产及其他经济利益。对承受国有土地使用权应支付的土地出让金，要征收契税。不得因减免出让金而减免契税。<br>

<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>『得分关键』对免税单位无偿使用纳税单位的土地(如公安、海关等单位使用铁路、民航等单位的土地)，免征城镇土地使用税；对纳税单位无偿使用免税单位的土地，纳税单位应照章缴纳城镇土地使用税。<br>

<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>（1）将拥有的境内某处房产自1月1日起出租给境内甲居民企业，租期2年，每月不含税租金10万元，合同约定按季度支付。2024年甲企业实际支付租金90万元。<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>（2）将拥有的境内某处房产自1月1日起出租给境内乙居民企业，每年不含税租金240万元，租期到2025年底，2024年乙企业实际支付租金480万元。<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>（3）3月将拥有的境内某处房产转让给境内丙居民企业，不含税转让价格为3 400万元，该房产原值为2 000万元，已按税法规定计提折旧600万元。<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>（4）5月销售一台设备给境内丁居民企业并提供安装和技术指导服务，合同约定不含税金额共800万元，款项12月已支付，未单独列明服务的收费金额，且无相同或相近业务的计价标准。当地主管税务机关按照税法规定的最低标准核定，该劳务的计税收入指定丁企业为扣缴义务人。<br>

<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>『得分关键』非居民企业出租位于中国境内的房屋、建筑物等不动产，对未在中国境内设立机构、场所进行日常管理的，以其取得的租金收入全额计算缴纳企业所得税，由中国境内的承租人在每次支付或到期应支付时代扣代缴。<br>

『正确答案』D<br>
『答案解析』丁企业应代扣代缴的企业所得税＝800×10％×10％＝8（万元）。<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>『得分关键』非居民企业与中国居民企业签订机器设备或货物销售合同，同时提供设备安装、装配、技术培训、指导、监督服务等劳务，其销售货物合同中未列明提供上述劳务服务收费金额，或者计价不合理的，主管税务机关可以根据实际情况，参照相同或相近业务的计价标准核定劳务收入。无参照标准的，以不低于销售货物合同总价款的10％为原则，确定非居民企业的劳务收入。<br>

<br><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span><strong>四、综合分析题</strong><br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>1.某家电制造企业为增值税一般纳税人，属于小型微利企业。2024年度企业资产总额为4 900万元，实现营业收入9 000万元、投资收益500万元、其他收益20万元，发生营业成本5 800万元、税金及附加160万元、管理费用1 400万元、销售费用1 000万元、财务费用40万元、营业外支出190万元、资产处置收益－55.6万元。2024年度该企业自行计算的会计利润为874.4万元。2025年4月该企业进行2024年企业所得税汇算清缴时，聘请了某会计师事务所进行审核，发现其2024年发生如下事项：<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>（1）1月租入一间门面房，合同约定租期6年，按年支付每年不含增值税租金10万元，企业2024年就该合同未计算缴纳印花税。<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>（2）4月购入一套收藏用的清代檀香家具，成本费用中含2024年已计提的折旧200万元。<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>（3）财务费用中含满足扣除条件的向与企业无关联关系的自然人以8％利率支付的借款利息支出20万元，金融企业同期同类贷款利率为6％。<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>（4）销售费用中含为股东报销与企业业务无关的个人消费10万元。<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>（5）投资收益含逾期理财本期收回收益，转回上年已计提资产减值准备100万元。<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>（6）企业当年职工人数为290人，全年成本费用中含实际发放的合理工资总额3 000万元，发生职工福利费450万元、职工教育经费90万元、拨缴的工会经费40万元。上年结转未扣除的职工教育经费50万元。<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>（7）研发费用中含研发人员人工费用200万元、直接投入费用500万元、折旧费用20万元、其他相关费用90万元。<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>（8）6月底将一台安全生产专用设备转让给C公司，取得不含税转让价款120万元。该专用设备（属于企业所得税优惠目录规定范围）于2022年6月底购入并当月投入使用，取得的增值税专用发票注明金额200万元、税额26万元，会计和税法均采用年限平均法计提折旧，该企业2022年已享受税额抵免优惠。<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>（注：财产租赁合同印花税税率为1‰，各扣除项目均在汇算清缴期取得有效凭证。）<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>要求：根据上述资料，回答下列问题。<br>

『正确答案』ABC<br>
『答案解析』选项A，企业购买的文物、艺术品用于收藏、展示、保值增值的，作为投资资产进行税务处理，文物、艺术品资产在持有期间，计提的折旧、摊销费用，不得税前扣除，清代檀香家具计提的折旧调增应纳税所得额200万元。选项B，利息支出纳税调整增加额＝20－20÷8％×6％＝5（万元）。选项C，为股东报销与企业业务无关的个人消费，不得税前扣除，销售费用调增应纳税所得额10万元。选项D，计提资产减值准备不得税前扣除，计提时已纳税调增，转回上年已计提资产减值准备应调减应纳税所得额100万元。选项E，其他相关费用扣除限额＝（200＋500＋20）÷（1－10％）×10％＝80（万元），实际发生90万元，按80万元计算税前加计扣除数额。研发费用加计扣除额＝（200＋500＋20＋80）×100％＝800（万元）。<br>

<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>2.中国居民刘某为境内某科技公司研究员，2024年度涉税事项和收入信息如下：<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>（1）每月从任职公司取得工资收入18 500元（含按国家标准缴纳的“三险一金”3 500元）。<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>（2）将直辖市一套住房出租给当地工作的夏某居住，签订的租赁合同约定，租期为一年，每月不含税租金为3 800元，租金按季度支付，合同签订日和房屋交付日均为6月30日，合同生效日为7月1日。不考虑除房产税、印花税以外的税费，享受“六税两费”减半税收优惠。<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>（3）9月承接境外一项咨询业务，一次性取得咨询费收入折合人民币80 000元，已经依法扣缴个人所得税12 000元。<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>（4）12月通过红十字会捐款44 400元。<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>（注：刘某每月享受的专项附加扣除金额为3 000元，境内工资所得已足额预扣预缴税款5 880元，公益慈善捐赠选择在综合所得年度汇算清缴时扣除。不考虑国际税收协定因素。）<br>

<script type="text/javascript">
    var handleQuestionClick= function(jyID, videoID,status) {
        var cwareID = pageData.cwareID;
        var dyForumID = pageData.dyForumID;
        var cwID = pageData.cwID;
        var homeSubjectID = pageData.homeSubjectID;
        if (status == null || status == "") {
            status = 2;
        }
        if (status == 2) {//未报课，跳转到免费答疑页面
            var url = "//member.chinaacc.com/faq/free/lecture/query.shtm?Forum_ID=" + dyForumID + "&qclass=b0015&QNo=" + jyID + "&cwareID=" + cwareID;
            url += "&Jy_url=[KCJYGET," + cwareID + "," + videoID + "," + jyID + ",ISNEW]";
            url += "&identity=" + homeSubjectID;
            window.open(url);
        } else {
            var url = "//member.chinaacc.com/faq/interface/faqView.shtm?cwID=" + cwID + "&qclass=b0015&QNo=" + jyID;
            url += "&Jy_url=[KCJYGET," + cwareID + "," + videoID + "," + jyID + ",ISNEW]";
            url += "&identity=" + homeSubjectID;
            window.open(url);
        }
    }

    function openAiFaqWithLecture(jyID, videoID) {
        const aiFaqMenuItem = document.getElementById('click_aiFaq');
        if (!aiFaqMenuItem) return;

        // 1. 展开“提问”面板
        if (!$(aiFaqMenuItem).hasClass('on')) {
            $(aiFaqMenuItem).trigger('click');
        }

        // 2. 准备参数
        const cwareID = pageData.cwareID;
        const cwID = pageData.cwID;
        const subjectId = pageData.cwareSubjectID;
        const majorID = pageData.cwareEduID;

        const faqUrl = "https://member.chinaacc.com/aiFaq/miniFaq?" +
            $.param({
                topicID: null,
                majorID: majorID,
                subjectId: subjectId,
                cwID: cwID,
                cwareID: cwareID,
                videoID: videoID,
                jyID: jyID,
                isLive: 0
            });

        // 3. 更新 iframe 的 src（即使已加载也刷新，确保内容更新）
        const $frame = $("#aiFaqFrame");
        $frame.attr("src", faqUrl).data("loaded", true);
    }
</script>

<script>
	var showPointTest = function (pointVideoLen, pointOpenType) {
		window.testController.showPoint4Click(pointVideoLen, pointOpenType);
	}

	var closeTest = function () {
	}

	var csPop = function (el,nodeID,userID,cwareID,videoID) {
		var cwareID = pageData.cwareID;
		var videoID = pageData.videoID;
        $.getJSON(pageData.basePath+'/testPop/getPointFlag.shtm',{
            cwareID:cwareID,
            videoID:videoID,
            r:Math.random()
        },function(data){
			// 控制div显示（0 都不显示设置选项，1 都显示显示，2 显示知识点测试，3 显示单元测试）
			var test = data[0];
			console.log(test);
			// 两个设置选项
			var setPointTest = $('#setPointTest');
			var setUnitTest = $('#setUnitTest');
			switch (test.settingFlag) {
				case 1:
					setPointTest.show();
					setUnitTest.show();
					break;
				case 2:
					setPointTest.show();
					setUnitTest.hide();
					break;
				case 3:
					setPointTest.hide();
					setUnitTest.show();
					break;
				default:
					setPointTest.hide();
					setUnitTest.hide();
					break;
			}
            $("#zPopFlag1").addClass("on");
            $("#dPopFlag1").addClass("on");
			$("#tPopFlag1").addClass("on");

            for (var i = 0, len = data.length; i < len; i++) {
                var test = data[i];
                var currOpenType = test.pointOpenType;
                switch (currOpenType) {
                    case "z": //知识点测试
                        var chickID = test.pointFlag == 0?"zPopFlag0":"zPopFlag1"
                        $("#"+chickID).addClass("on").siblings('li').removeClass('on');
                        break;
                    case "d": //单元测试
                        var chickID = test.pointFlag == 0?"dPopFlag0":"dPopFlag1"
                        $("#"+chickID).addClass("on").siblings('li').removeClass('on');
                        break;
					case "t": //知识点练习
						var chickID = test.pointFlag == 0?"tPopFlag0":"tPopFlag1"
						$("#"+chickID).addClass("on").siblings('li').removeClass('on');
						break;
                    default :
                        $("#zPopFlag1").addClass("on");
                        $("#dPopFlag1").addClass("on");
                        $("#tPopFlag1").addClass("on");
                        break;
                }
            }

        });
		var _this = $("." + el);
		var myHeight = _this.height();
		_this.css("marginTop", -myHeight / 2)
		$(".mask").show();
		_this.show();
	}

</script><div id="aiFaq" style="display:none;width:100%;height:100%;">
                    <iframe id="aiFaqFrame" style="width: 100%; height: 100%; border: none; margin: 0; padding: 0; overflow: hidden;" frameborder="0" scrolling="no">
                    </iframe>
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>
    </div>

    function clearEditImgData() {

<script src="/xcware/cwresources/js/lib/require.js?bust=2.1.13.9" data-main="/xcware/cwresources/js/main/h5video/h5VideoPlayApp20190813.js?bust=2.1.13.9">

<script type="text/javascript">
$(document).ready(function(){
	var tpjb = false;
	if (tpjb) {
		var tpjbtime=window.setInterval(function(){ 
			if (window.cdelvideo.flashapi.getMediaStatus() == "play"
				&& $(".menu .pjqp .pop").css('display') == 'none') {
					$(".menu .pjqp .pop").stop(true,true).fadeIn();
					var tpjbtimeout=window.setTimeout(function(){
						$(".menu .pjqp .pop").stop(true,true).fadeOut();
						window.clearTimeout(tpjbtime);
					}, 1000 * 4);
				}
		}, 1000 * 1);

	}
	
	//var refreshuserid=window.setInterval(function(){ 
	//	refreshsid();
	//}, 1000 * 60 * 30);
	$("#click_lecture").one('click', function() {
    // 使用 setTimeout 延时 200ms 执行
    setTimeout(function() {
        // 补丁：点击讲义时定位到当前讲义位置
        window.jyView.selectLecture(window.jyView.getCurrJyID());
    }, 300); // 200 毫秒延时
});
	
	
	var statusCode = $("#statusCode").val();
	var isTy = $("#isTy").val();
	var tjcwareID = $("#tjcwareID").val();
    var tjvideoID = $("#tjvideoID").val();
    
    if(isTy == '1' && statusCode == '2'){
    	var videoLen = $("#videoLen").val();
    	var showFlag = true;
    	var completeTimer=window.setInterval(function(){ 
    		var time = window.cdelvideo.flashapi.getNowPlayingTime();
    		if(Math.abs(videoLen - time) < 4 && showFlag){
    			showFlag = false;
    			completePlay();
    		}
    	}, 1000 * 1);
	}

    
	if(statusCode == '1' && isTy =='0' && tjcwareID != '' && tjvideoID != ''){
		var teacherHideTime = new Date().getTime();//上次隐藏老师时间
		var pauseTime = new Date().getTime();//上次暂停时间
		var speedTime = new Date().getTime();//上次超过一倍速播放时间
		var openTimeLine = 1000 * 60 * 5;//5分钟弹出
		var openTimeLinePause = 1000 * 3;//暂停3秒弹出
		
		var pointLen = $("#pointLen").val();
		var pointArr = pointLen.split(',');
		var playPointNum = 0;
		var playSeekNum = 0;
		var nowPlayTime = 0;
		var videoShowUpdate = window.setInterval(function(){ 
			var openTip = $("#openTip").val();//0弹框 1不弹
			//暂停触发being
			var now = new Date().getTime();
			if (window.cdelvideo.flashapi.getMediaStatus() == "pause"){
				if(now - pauseTime > openTimeLinePause && openTip == '0'){
					openTip = '1';
					courseUpgrade('courseUpgrade-experience');
				}
			}
			if (window.cdelvideo.flashapi.getMediaStatus() == "play"){
				pauseTime = new Date().getTime();
			}
			//暂停触发end
			//隐藏老师触发begin
			if(window.cdelvideo.flashapi.getIsHideTeacher() == '1'){//隐藏
				if(openTip == '0' && now - teacherHideTime > openTimeLine){
					//alert('隐藏老师弹出');
					openTip = '1';
					var tyData = $("#tyData").val();
					courseUpgradePrompt('courseUpgrade-prompt');
				}
			}else{//未隐藏
				teacherHideTime = new Date().getTime();
			}
			//隐藏老师触发end
			
			//倍速触发begin
			 if(window.cdelvideo.flashapi.getCurrentSpeed() > 1){//隐藏
				if(openTip == '0' && now - speedTime > openTimeLine){
					openTip = '1';
					courseUpgradePrompt('courseUpgrade-prompt');
				}
			}else{//未隐藏
				speedTime = new Date().getTime();
			} 
			//倍速触发
			//学习时间
			var time = window.cdelvideo.flashapi.getNowPlayingTime();
			
			if(openTip == '0'){
				if(time - nowPlayTime > 5 && nowPlayTime > 0){
					playSeekNum ++;
					if(playSeekNum > 1){
						openTip = '1';
						courseUpgradePrompt('courseUpgrade-prompt');
					}
				}
			}
			nowPlayTime = time;
			$("#openTip").val(openTip);
		}, 1000 * 1);
	}
// 	TODO 初始化页面 需要加载观看人数
	initStydyNums();
});
// 初始化学习人数
function initStydyNums() {
	var cwareID = pageData.cwareID;
	var videoID = pageData.videoID;
	postAesData({
		data: {
			params: {
				"cwareID": cwareID,
				"videoID": videoID
			},
			domain: "chinaacc",
			resourcePath: "+/innercware/service/getCwareVisitCount",
			af: "1",
			ap: "pc"
		},
		// ajax成功回调
		success: function (data) {
			if (data.success) {
				if (data.result.show == 1) {
					$(".stydyNums").text(data.result.countForPaid + "人已学习");
				}
			}
		}
	});
}
function courseUpgradePrompt(id) {
    var _main = $('.'+ id);
    _main.show().css('margin-left',-(_main.width()/2));
    //退出全屏
    if(document.exitFullscreen) {
        document.exitFullscreen();
    } else if(document.mozCancelFullScreen) {
        document.mozCancelFullScreen();
    } else if(document.webkitExitFullscreen) {
        document.webkitExitFullscreen();
    } else if(document.msExitFullscreen) {
        document.msExitFullscreen();
    }
}

function showTjVideo(id, dm,category, context){
	var statusCode = $("#statusCode").val();
	var experienceProductId = $("#openProductId").val();
	var lowShiftsProductId = $("#lowShiftsProductId").val();
	var subject =  $("#subject").val();
	var tjcwareID = $("#tjcwareID").val();
    var tjvideoID = $("#tjvideoID").val();
    track(dm, category, context);
	if(statusCode == '1'){//有体验资格没有升级资格
		$.getJSON("http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/video/h5video/openClass.shtm?experienceProductId="+experienceProductId+"&lowShiftsProductId="+lowShiftsProductId,
		  	     function(data){
		  		   if(data.success != undefined && data.success){//开课成功
		  			 window.cdelvideo.flashapi.pauseVideo();
		  			 //closeCourseUpgrade(id);
		  			 var url = 'http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/video/h5video/videoPlay.shtm?cwareID='+tjcwareID+'&videoID='+tjvideoID;
		  			 window.open(url,"_blank");
		  		  }else{
		  			 window.cdelvideo.flashapi.pauseVideo();
		  			 //closeCourseUpgrade(id);
		  			 alert('开通体验课失败');
		  		  }
		});
	}else{
		window.cdelvideo.flashapi.pauseVideo();
		//closeCourseUpgrade(id);
		var url = 'http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/video/h5video/videoPlay.shtm?cwareID='+tjcwareID+'&videoID='+tjvideoID;
		window.open(url,"_blank");
	}
}

function courseUpgrade(id) {
    var _main = $('.'+ id);
    _main.parents('.courseUpgrade-mod').show();
    _main.show().css('margin-top',-(_main.height()/2)).siblings('.courseUpgrade-main').hide();
    if(document.exitFullscreen) {
        document.exitFullscreen();
    } else if(document.mozCancelFullScreen) {
        document.mozCancelFullScreen();
    } else if(document.webkitExitFullscreen) {
        document.webkitExitFullscreen();
    } else if(document.msExitFullscreen) {
        document.msExitFullscreen();
    }
}
//closeCourseUpgrade(id,callback)  id 关闭弹窗的id  callbackId 弹出确认弹窗id
function closeCourseUpgrade(id,callbackId, dm, category, context){
    var _main = $('.'+ id);
    _main.hide().css('margin-top',0).parents('.courseUpgrade-mod').hide();
    if(callbackId && callbackId != ''){
        courseUpgrade(callbackId)
    }
    track(dm, category, context);
}

function completePlay(){
	var statusCode = $("#statusCode").val();
	var isTy = $("#isTy").val();
	if(statusCode == '2' && isTy == '1'){
		window.cdelvideo.flashapi.pauseVideo();
		courseUpgrade('courseUpgrade-upgrade');
	}
}

function playNext(dm, category, context){
	window.cdelvideo.flashapi.playVideo();
	closeCourseUpgrade('courseUpgrade-upgrade');
	track(dm, category, context);
}

function updateClass(dm, category, context){
	var upgradeClassID = $("#upgradeClassID").val();
	var details = $("#details").val();
	var url = 'http://sale.chinaacc.com/newweb/upgrade/upgradeInfo.shtm?viewClassId=' + upgradeClassID + '&detailIds=' + details;
	window.open(url,"_blank");
	closeCourseUpgrade('courseUpgrade-upgrade');
	track(dm, category, context);
}

	courseUpgrade('courseUpgrade-twshow');
}

function jyqxInfo(){
	courseUpgrade('courseUpgrade-jyqx');
}

function askktty(id){
	var statusCode = $("#statusCode").val();
	var experienceProductId = $("#openProductId").val();
	var lowShiftsProductId = $("#lowShiftsProductId").val();
	var subject =  $("#subject").val();
	var tjcwareID = $("#tjcwareID").val();
    var tjvideoID = $("#tjvideoID").val();
	if(statusCode == '1'){//有体验资格没有升级资格
		$.getJSON("http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/video/h5video/openClass.shtm?experienceProductId="+experienceProductId+"&lowShiftsProductId="+lowShiftsProductId,
		  	     function(data){
		  		   if(data.success != undefined && data.success){//开课成功
		  			 closeCourseUpgrade(id);
		  			 courseUpgrade('courseUpgrade-result');
		  		  }else{
		  			 alert('开通体验课失败');
		  		  }
		});
	} 
}

function askktty_result(id){
	closeCourseUpgrade(id);
	var url=basePath+"/faqNew/faqAsk.shtm";
	var jyID = $("#jyID").val();
	var cwareID = $("#cwareID").val();
	var videoID = $("#videoID").val();
	var title = $("#title").val();
	var content = $("#askContent").val();
	var Jy_url="[KCJYGET,"+cwareID+","+videoID+","+jyID+",ISNEW]";
	$.post(url, {
		cwareID: cwareID,
		qclass: '100b',
		QNo: jyID,
		Jy_url: Jy_url,
		title: title,
		content: content
	},function(data){ 
		var result = eval("(" + data + ")");
		if(result["flag"] == true){$("#title").val("");
			$("#askContent").val("");
			window.faqvideoPlay._winAlert("提示信息","提问成功,您可以在播放器下方的答疑区查看您的提问!");
			window.cdelvideo.flashapi.playVideo();
			//显示提问信息
			window.faqvideoPlay.faqAllAsk(1);
			//关闭窗口
			window.newpage._closeItem(window.newpage);
		}else{
			$("#title").val("");
			$("#askContent").val("");
			window.faqvideoPlay._winAlert("错误信息",result["msg"]);
			window.cdelvideo.flashapi.playVideo();
			//关闭窗口
			window.newpage._closeItem(window.newpage);
		}
		// 剩余文字初始化
		$("#askContent").trigger("propertychange");
		$("#askContent").trigger("input");
	});
}

function jyqx(id){
	var statusCode = $("#statusCode").val();
	var experienceProductId = $("#openProductId").val();
	var lowShiftsProductId = $("#lowShiftsProductId").val();
	var subject =  $("#subject").val();
	var tjcwareID = $("#tjcwareID").val();
    var tjvideoID = $("#tjvideoID").val();
	if(statusCode == '1'){//有体验资格没有升级资格
		$.getJSON("http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/video/h5video/openClass.shtm?experienceProductId="+experienceProductId+"&lowShiftsProductId="+lowShiftsProductId,
		  	     function(data){
		  		   if(data.success != undefined && data.success){//开课成功
		  			 closeCourseUpgrade(id);
		  			 showMemoryDiv();
		  		  }else{
		  			 alert('开通体验课失败');
		  		  }
		});
	} 
}

function pointTest(){
	var statusCode = $("#statusCode").val();
	var isTy = $("#isTy").val();
	var tjcwareID = $("#tjcwareID").val();
    var tjvideoID = $("#tjvideoID").val();
	var openTip = $("#openTip").val();
	var playPointNum = $("#playPointNum").val();
	playPointNum++;
	if(openTip == '0' && playPointNum > 2 && (statusCode == '1'||statusCode == '2') && isTy =='0' && tjcwareID != '' && tjvideoID != ''){
		courseUpgradePrompt('courseUpgrade-prompt');
		$("#openTip").val('1');
	}
	$("#playPointNum").val(playPointNum);
}


function track(dm, category, context) {
	if(category != undefined && context != undefined && dm != undefined){
		CDELTracker.$track(dm, {
			"category" : category,
			"context" : context
		});
	}
}

//判断sid是否有效，无效时进行踢出登录
function refreshsid(){
	$.getJSON("//elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/video/userSession/refresh.shtm",
	  	 function(data){ 
		   if(data.code != undefined && data.code == -1){//登录状态失效 
			   window.location.href = "//elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/error.jsp?userFlag=3";
	  		}
	});
}

// 触发埋点功能方法
function buried(dm) {
	var cwareID = $("#cwareID").val(); // 课件编号
	var videoID = $("#videoID").val(); // 视频编号
	var cwareEduID = $("#cwareEduID").val(); // 辅导id
	var subject = $("#subject").val(); // 科目id
	CDELTracker.$track(dm, {
		"$custom_cwareID" : cwareID,
		"$custom_videoID" : videoID,
		"$custom_cwareEduID" : cwareEduID,
		"$custom_cwareSubjectID" : subject
	});
}

	buried(this);
});

	buried(this);
});

$('.eyeColorBox ul li').click(function (){
	var smallColorClass = $(this).attr('data-color');
	$(this).parents('eyeMode').find('a').removeClass(smallColorClass);
	$(this).addClass('on').siblings('li').removeClass('on');
	$('.eyeHoverBtn').removeClass('changeBlue changeYellow changeGreen').addClass(smallColorClass);
	$('.splitsWrap ,#lecture').removeClass('changeBlue changeYellow changeGreen').addClass(smallColorClass);
	setCookies("eyeModeIndex",$(this).index());
	setCookies("eyeModeColor",smallColorClass);
})


function setCookies(name,value)
{
	var Days = 1;
	var exp  = new Date();
	exp.setTime(exp.getTime() + Days*30*60*1000);
	document.cookie = name + "="+ escape(value) +";domain=chinaacc.com;path=/;";
}


function getCookie2(name){
	var strcookie = document.cookie;//获取cookie字符串
	var arrcookie = strcookie.split("; ");//分割
	//遍历匹配
	for ( var i = 0; i < arrcookie.length; i++) {
		var arr = arrcookie[i].split("=");
		if (arr[0] == name){
			return arr[1];
		}
	}
	return "";
}

//写个方法判断是否缩放导致的滚动条位置变化
function setIsScaleScroll(){
	window.isScaleScroll = true;
	clearTimeout($.data(this, 'scaleTimer'));
	$.data(this, 'scaleTimer', setTimeout(function() {
		window.isScaleScroll = false;
	}, 500));
}

		//字体切换 //字体放大缩小
$(".setFontNormal a").click(function () {
	var _type = $(this)[0].id;
	var bl = $(".lectureCon .memoDiv b,.memoDiv .showIsAnswer");
	var allItem = $(".lectureCon li,td");
	//ai智能看逐字稿
	let aiTranscriptDiv = $("#aiTranscript");
	switch (_type) {
		case 'bigger':
			var fontSize = [];
			for (var i = 0; i < allItem.length; i++) {
				var _item = $(allItem[i]);
				var _size = parseInt(_item.css("font-size").split("px")[0])
				//console.log(_size)
				_item.css({"font-size": (_size + 1) + "px"});
				bl.css({"font-size": (_size + 1) + "px"})
				fontSize.push(_size + 1);
			}
			setUserFontSize(fontSize);
			if($(".font14zd") && $(".font14zd").css("font-size")){
				var redSize = parseInt($(".font14zd").css("font-size").split("px")[0]);
				$(".font14zd").css({"font-size": (redSize + 1) + "px"});
			}
			if($(".fontKaiti") && $(".fontKaiti").css("font-size")){
				var redSize = parseInt($(".fontKaiti").css("font-size").split("px")[0]);
				$(".fontKaiti").css({"font-size": (redSize + 1) + "px"});
			}
			//ai智能看逐字稿
			if(aiTranscriptDiv.length > 0){
				let aiFontSize = parseInt(aiTranscriptDiv.css("font-size").split("px")[0]);
				aiTranscriptDiv.css({"font-size": (aiFontSize + 1) + "px"});
			}
			//判断是否缩放导致的滚动条位置变化
			setIsScaleScroll();
			break;
		case 'normal':
			allItem.css({"font-size": "14px"});
			var allItemTd = $(".lectureCon td");
			allItemTd.css({"font-size": "12px"});
			setUserFontSize([16,12]);
			bl.css({"font-size": "14px"});
			$(".lectureCon .font14").css({"font-size": "14px"});
			$(".lectureCon .font16").css({"font-size": "16px"});
			if($(".font14zd") && $(".font14zd").css("font-size")){
				$(".font14zd").css({"font-size": "14px"});
			}
			if($(".font16zd")){
				$(".font16zd").css({"font-size": "16px"});
			}
			if($(".fontKaiti")){
				$(".fontKaiti").css({"font-size": "15px"});
			}
			//ai智能看逐字稿
			if(aiTranscriptDiv.length > 0){
				aiTranscriptDiv.css({"font-size": "14px"});
			}
			//判断是否缩放导致的滚动条位置变化
			setIsScaleScroll();
			break;
		case 'smaller':
			if (allItem.css("font-size") == "10px") {
				return;
			}
			var fontSize = [];
			for (var i = 0; i < allItem.length; i++) {
				var _item = $(allItem[i]);
				var _size = parseInt(_item.css("font-size").split("px")[0])
				_item.css({"font-size": (_size - 1) + "px"});
				bl.css({"font-size": (_size - 1) + "px"});
				fontSize.push(_size - 1);
			}
			setUserFontSize(fontSize);
			if($(".font14zd") && $(".font14zd").css("font-size")){
				var redSize = parseInt($(".font14zd").css("font-size").split("px")[0]);
				$(".font14zd").css({"font-size": (redSize - 1) + "px"});
			}
			if($(".fontKaiti") && $(".fontKaiti").css("font-size")){
				var redSize = parseInt($(".fontKaiti").css("font-size").split("px")[0]);
				$(".fontKaiti").css({"font-size": (redSize - 1) + "px"});
			}
			//ai智能看逐字稿
			if(aiTranscriptDiv.length > 0){
				let aiFontSize = parseInt(aiTranscriptDiv.css("font-size").split("px")[0]);
				aiTranscriptDiv.css({"font-size": (aiFontSize - 1) + "px"});
			}
			//判断是否缩放导致的滚动条位置变化
			setIsScaleScroll();
			break;
	}

})

var myNotePop = function (el,nodeID,userID,pictureUrls) {
	$("#nodeID").val(nodeID);
	$("#userID").val(userID);
	var _this = $("." + el);
	var myHeight = _this.height();
	_this.css("marginTop", -myHeight / 2)
	$(".mask").show();
	_this.show();
	if (el === "notesModify") {
		var _textarea = $(".textAreaBox textarea" )
		_textarea.val("");
		_textarea.val($("#modify_" + nodeID).text());
		$(".textAreaBox i").text(_textarea.val().toString().trim().length+'/800');
		console.log(pictureUrls)
		var pic = pictureUrls.split(",");
		$(".notesModify .picBox-more").show();
		$(".notesModify #pic-list").html("")
		for(var j=0;j<pic.length;j++){
			if (pic[j]!=''){
				$(".notesModify #pic-list").append("<a href=\"javascript:void(0)\" class=\"picBox-img\"><span onclick=\"myNotePicPop('"+pic[j]+"')\"><img src=\""+pic[j]+"\"></span><i class=\"close\"></i></a>");
			}
		}
		$(".notesModify .picBox-img .close").on('click', function() {
			$(this).parent(".picBox-img").remove();
			if ($(".notesModify #pic-list").children("a").length<3&&$(".notesModify .picBox-more").is(":hidden")){
				$(".notesModify .picBox-more").show();
			}
			$('.notesModify .picBox-num em').html($(".notesModify #pic-list").children("a").length);
		})
		if ($(".notesModify #pic-list").children("a").length>=3){
			$(".notesModify .picBox-more").hide();
		}
		$('.notesModify .picBox-num em').html($(".notesModify #pic-list").children("a").length);
	}
}

	//_this.find(".pic").css("margin-top", - _this.find(".pic").height() / 2);
	//_this.find(".pic").css("margin-left", - _this.find(".pic").width() / 2);
}

	url = url.replace("_chg","");

	_this.css("background-color", "white");//加上白色背景防止思维导图黑色字体看不见

	_this.css("height", "500px");
	_this.find(".pic").attr("src",url);
	_this.find(".pic").css("max-width", "900px");
	_this.find(".pic").css("max-height", "500px");
	$(".mask-pic").show();
	_this.show();
}

var closeMyNotePop = function (el,e) {
	$("."+el).hide();
	if (el == 'amplifyPicPop') {
		$(".mask-pic").hide();
	}else{
		$(".mask").hide();
	}
	if (el ==="deleteNote" &&  e ==="1"){
		$(".deleteBox").hide();
		var nodeID = $("#nodeID").val();
		var userID = $("#userID").val();
		var cwareID = $("#cwareID").val();
		noteDel(nodeID,userID,cwareID);
	}

}
var modifyUploadFile = function () {
	$("#modifyUploadFile").click();
}
$("#modifyUploadFile").on("change",function (e) {
	var e = e
	//获取 文件 个数 取消的时候使用
	var files = e.target.files;
	if(files.length>0){
		for(var i=0;i<files.length;i++){
			//调用上传图片方法
			modifyUploadImg(files[i]);
		}
	}
});
var modifyUploadImg = function (file) {
	var time = this.toDateTimeStr2(new Date());
	$.get(pageData.basePath+"/upload/getMd5Code.shtm?str="+time+"&cwareID="+pageData.cwareID,function(data){
		if(data === ""){
			alert("上传错误")
		}else{
			var fd = new FormData();
			fd.append("files",file);
			fd.append('origin', "CWARE");
			fd.append('time', time);
			fd.append("securecode", data);
			$.ajax({
				url: pageData.basePath+"/upload/image.shtm?cwareID="+pageData.cwareID,
				type: 'POST',
				async: false,
				contentType: false,
				processData: false,
				dataType: 'json',
				data: fd,
				success: function(data){
					if(data.code==0){
						// alert("图片上传成功!");
						$(".notesModify #pic-list").append("<a href=\"javascript:void(0)\" class=\"picBox-img\"><span onclick=\"myNotePicPop('"+data.imageUrl+"')\"><img src=\""+data.imageUrl+"\"></span><i class=\"close\"></i></a>");
						if ($(".notesModify #pic-list").children("a").length==3){
							$(".notesModify .picBox-more").hide();
						}
						$(".notesModify .picBox-img .close").on('click', function() {
							console.log(2222)
							$(this).parent(".picBox-img").remove();
							if ($(".notesModify #pic-list").children("a").length<3&&$(".notesModify .picBox-more").is(":hidden")){
								$(".notesModify .picBox-more").show();
							}
							$('.notesModify .picBox-num em').html($(".notesModify #pic-list").children("a").length);
						})
						$('.notesModify .picBox-num em').html($(".notesModify #pic-list").children("a").length);
					}else{
						alert(data.msg);
					}
				},
			});
		}
	})
}

function toDateTimeStr2(intTime){
	var date;
	if(intTime == null){
		date = new Date();
	}else{
		date = new Date(intTime);
	}
	var month = date.getMonth() + 1;
	if(month < 10){
		month = "0" + month;
	}
	var day = date.getDate();
	if(day < 10){
		day = "0" + day;
	}
	var hours = date.getHours();
	if(hours < 10){
		hours = "0" + hours;
	}
	var m = date.getMinutes();
	if(m < 10){
		m = "0" + m;
	}
	var s = date.getSeconds();
	if(s < 10){
		s = "0" + s;
	}
	return date.getFullYear() + "-" + month + "-" + day + " " + hours + ":" + m + ":" + s;
};

var noteDel  = function(nodeID,userID,cwareID){
	var basePath = pageData.basePath;
	/*if(!confirm("您确定要删除该条笔记吗?")) {
		return false;
	}*/
	$.post(basePath+"/viewNode/load/delViewNote.shtm", {
		nodeID : nodeID,
		userID : userID,
		cwareID : cwareID,
		r:Math.random()
	},function(data){
		var result = eval("(" + data + ")");
		if(result >0){
			alert("删除成功!");
			init();
		}else{
			alert("删除失败！");
		}
	});
}
$(".textAreaBox textarea").bind('input propertychange',function (){
	let trim =  $(".textAreaBox textarea").val().trim();
	var textAreaBox_i = $(".textAreaBox i")
	if (trim.toString().length>800){
		textAreaBox_i.css("color","red");
	}else{
		textAreaBox_i.css("color","#999");
	}
	textAreaBox_i.text(trim.toString().length+'/800');
})
var submitNote = function () {
	closeMyNotePop("notesModify","0")
	var nodeID = $("#nodeID").val();
	var userID = $("#userID").val();
	var cwareID = $("#cwareID").val();
	var videoID = $("#videoID").val();
	var picStr = "";
	if ($(".notesModify .picBox-img span img").length>0){
		for (var i = 0;i<$(".notesModify .picBox-img span img").length;i++){
			if (i==($(".notesModify .picBox-img span img").length-1)){
				picStr = picStr + $(".notesModify .picBox-img span img")[i].src;
			}else {
				picStr = picStr + $(".notesModify .picBox-img span img")[i].src+",";
			}
		}
	}
	noteUpdateSubmit(nodeID,userID,cwareID,videoID,picStr);

}
//笔记修改保存
var  noteUpdateSubmit = function(nodeID,userID,cwareID,videoID,pictureUrls){
	var basePath = pageData.basePath;
	var nodeContent = $(".textAreaBox textarea" ).val();
	if(nodeContent.length>800){
		alert("内容过长，最多输入800字 ！");
		return;
	}
	$.post(basePath+"/viewNode/load/addViewNote.shtm", {
		nodeID:nodeID,
		cwareID:cwareID,
		videoID:videoID,
		nodeContent:nodeContent,
		pictureUrls:pictureUrls,
		r:Math.random()

	}, function(data) {
		var result = eval("(" + data + ")");
		if(result >0){
			alert("保存成功！");
			init();

		}else{
			alert("保存失败！");
		}
	});
}

//初始化加载方法
var init = function(){
	//初始化显示当前视频笔记
	var basePath = pageData.basePath;
	var statPath = pageData.statPath;
	var cwareID = pageData.cwareID;
	var videoID = pageData.videoID;
	var iconUrl = pageData.iconUrl;
	var tableStr = "";
	$.getJSON(basePath+"/viewNode/load/getAllNoteList.shtm",{
		cwareID:cwareID,
		videoID:videoID,
		r:Math.random()
	},function(data){
		var obj = data;
		var dataLen = obj.length;
		if(dataLen>0){
			tableStr += "<ul>";
			for(var i=0;i<dataLen;i++){
				tableStr += "<li><span id='modify_"+obj[i].nodeID+"'>"+obj[i].nodeContent+"</span>" ;
				var s = "<p class=\"noteConList\">"+"<span class='noteTime'>"+(obj[i].updateTime)+"</span>";
				s+= '<span style="margin-top: -25px;" class="buttonFunction fr">\n' +
						'<a href="javascript:void(0)" onClick="jumpVideo('+"'"+obj[i].nodeID+"'"+')" class="fontC"><i class="noteIcon icon01" ></i>收听相关课程</a>' +
						'<a href="javascript:void(0)" onClick="myNotePop(\'notesModify\','+"'"+obj[i].nodeID+"',"+"'"+obj[i].userID+"',"+"'"+obj[i].pictureUrls+"'"+')" class="fontC"><i class="noteIcon icon02" ></i>修改</a>' +
						'<a href="javascript:void(0)" onClick="myNotePop(\'deleteBox\','+"'"+obj[i].nodeID+"',"+"'"+obj[i].userID+"'"+')" class="fontC"><i class="noteIcon icon03" ></i>删除</a>' +
						'</span>';
				var reg = new RegExp("\n","g");
				tableStr +=s.replace(reg,"<br/>");
                tableStr +="</p>";
                if (obj[i].pictureUrls){
                    tableStr +="<div class='picBox clearfix'>";
                    var pic = obj[i].pictureUrls.split(",")
                    for(var j=0;j<pic.length;j++){
                        if (pic[j]!=''){
                            // pic[j] = "https://img.cdeledu.com/CWARE/2022/0111/561a3b15ff74ef66-0.png";
                            tableStr +="<a href='javascript:void(0)' class='picBox-img' onclick=\"window.note.myNotePicPop('"+pic[j]+"')\"><img src='"+pic[j]+"'></a>";
                        }
                    }
                    tableStr +="</div>";
                }
				tableStr +=" </li>";
			}
			tableStr +="</ul>";
		}else{
			tableStr +="<div class='tip tip_null'></div>";
		}
		$("#noteWrap").html(tableStr);
	});
}


function setUserFontSize(size){//设置用户字体大小的cookie
	var exdate=new Date();
	exdate.setDate(exdate.getDate()+60);
	document.cookie="userVideoLectureFontSize=" +escape(size)+ "; path=/xcware/" +";expires="+exdate.toGMTString();
}

//设置是否显示AI智能看的cookie（1为显示AI看，0为显示讲义，默认为0）
function setIsShowAiCookie(val){
	setCookies("isShowAiLook", val);
}
//获取是否显示AI智能看的cookie
function getIsShowAiCookie(){
	let isAiLook = 0;//默认显示讲义
	let isAiLookCookie = getCookie2("isShowAiLook");
	if (isAiLookCookie){
		isAiLook = isAiLookCookie;
	}
	return isAiLook;
}

//AI智能看、思维导图、同步讲义、全部讲义等按钮切换
function tabClick(divId){
	switch (divId){
		case "aizhinengkan":
			//ai看
			$("#toolsDiv").show();
			$("#lectureDiv").hide();
			$("#contentDiv").show();
			$("#aiTranscript").show();
			$("#mindMap").hide();
			$("#allLecture").hide();
			setIsShowAiCookie(1);
			break;
		case "siweidaotu":
			//思维导图
			$("#toolsDiv").hide();
			$("#aiTranscript").hide();
			$("#mindMap").show();
			$("#allLecture").hide();
			setIsShowAiCookie(0);
			break;
			//全部讲义
		case "quanbujiangi":
			$("#toolsDiv").show();
			$("#lectureDiv").show();
			$("#contentDiv").hide();
			$("#aiTranscript").hide();
			$("#mindMap").hide();
			$("#allLecture").show();
			setIsShowAiCookie(0);
			break;
		default:
			break;
	}
}
//AI智能看内容定位功能点击事件
$(".aiLocateMode a").click(function () {
	$(this).toggleClass("on");
	if($(this).hasClass("on")){
		//开启内容定位
		window.isScrollAi = true;
	}else{
		//关闭内容定位
		window.isScrollAi = false;
	}
});

$("#tryout .title .close").click(function () {
	$("#courseBox").stop(true).animate({right: "-360px"}, 200);
	$("#courseBox").removeClass("courseShow");
	$(".menu .menuCur").removeClass();
	$(".menu a.menuBack").remove();
	//$(".section").hide();
})
$(".set-tryout-box .set-con ul li").click(function () {
	$(this).addClass('on').siblings('li').removeClass('on')
})

function testFlag(flag, type) {
	window.testController.closePoint4Click();
	if(type == 'z') {
		pageData.pointZFlag = flag;
	}
	if(type == 'd') {
		pageData.pointDFlag = flag;
	}
	if(type == 't') {
		pageData.pointTFlag = flag;
	}
	var cwareID = pageData.cwareID;
	var videoID = pageData.videoID;
	var innerCwareID = pageData.innerCwareID;
	$.getJSON(pageData.basePath+'/testPop/updatePointFlag.shtm',{
		pointOpenType:type,
		pointFlag:flag,
		cwareID:cwareID,
		videoID:videoID,
		innerCwareID:innerCwareID,
		r:Math.random()
	},function(data){
		console.log(data)
	});
}

var closeCsPop = function (el) {
	window.testController.closePoint4Click();
	$("." + el).hide();
	$(".mask").hide();
}
